SELECT COUNT(*) FROM nesreca acdt_n, upravna_enota acdt_ue WHERE (acdt_n.upravna_enota = acdt_ue.id_upravna_enota) AND (acdt_n.vzrok_nesreca = 'PD') AND (acdt_n.opis_prizorisce = 'C');
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM nesreca acdt_n, upravna_enota acdt_ue WHERE (acdt_n.upravna_enota = acdt_ue.id_upravna_enota) AND (acdt_n.x_wgs84 < 15.72) AND (acdt_n.stanje_vozisce = 'SU');
